## Diagram 4

```mermaid
stateDiagram-v2
  [*] --> Init
  Init --> ParseArgs
  ParseArgs --> StageDecision
  StageDecision --> SetURLs: staging/test/other
  SetURLs --> PrepareActions
  PrepareActions --> RemoveOldFile
  RemoveOldFile --> PostOAuth
  PostOAuth --> GotToken
  GotToken --> GetLADs
  GetLADs --> GetLocations
  GetLocations --> [*]
```
